Data that is specific to a {\ttfamily gl\+Compressed\+Tex\+Image1D} or {\ttfamily gl\+Compressed\+Tex\+Image2D} call. The data is sent in the following order\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Render or Render\+Large header
\item Compressed\+Tex\+Image header
\end{DoxyItemize}

When a {\ttfamily gl\+Compressed\+Tex\+Image1D} call is made, the {\ttfamily height} field is not examined by the server and is considered padding. \mbox{\Hypertarget{glxproto_8h_a3c2ab3dfe67f7d0c4f58e11140ea30a9}\label{glxproto_8h_a3c2ab3dfe67f7d0c4f58e11140ea30a9}}

Data that is specifi to a {\ttfamily gl\+Compressed\+Tex\+Sub\+Image1D} or {\ttfamily gl\+Compressed\+Tex\+Sub\+Image2D} call. The data is sent in the following order\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Render or Render\+Large header
\item Compressed\+Tex\+Sub\+Image header
\end{DoxyItemize}

When a {\ttfamily gl\+Compressed\+Tex\+Sub\+Image1D} call is made, the {\ttfamily yoffset} and {\ttfamily height} fields are not examined by the server and are considered padding. \mbox{\Hypertarget{glxproto_8h_af256d6782f49ddba7f1a6b3bcf9dbf2b}\label{glxproto_8h_af256d6782f49ddba7f1a6b3bcf9dbf2b}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_render}{G\+L\+X\+Render}  \hyperlink{glxproto_8h_ad80e1352401b153884b5fca9f7307f14}{x\+G\+L\+X\+Render\+Req}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{glxproto_8h_a6419d0d1297025e220e3ac2b6de3fbef}\label{glxproto_8h_a6419d0d1297025e220e3ac2b6de3fbef}} 
\index{glxproto.\+h@{glxproto.\+h}!x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+R\+B\+Req@{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+R\+B\+Req}}
\index{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+R\+B\+Req@{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+R\+B\+Req}!glxproto.\+h@{glxproto.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+R\+B\+Req}{xGLXSetClientInfo2ARBReq}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_set_client_info2_a_r_b}{G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+RB}  \hyperlink{glxproto_8h_a6419d0d1297025e220e3ac2b6de3fbef}{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+R\+B\+Req}}

Protocol header for gl\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+RB

The gl\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+RB protocol differs from gl\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+RB in that the list of Open\+GL versions supported by the client is 3 {\ttfamily C\+A\+R\+D32} values per version\+: major version, minor version, and supported profile mask.

This protocol replaces {\ttfamily \hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_client_info}{G\+L\+X\+Client\+Info}} and {\ttfamily \hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_set_client_info_a_r_b}{G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+RB}}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_client_info}{G\+L\+X\+Client\+Info}, \hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_set_client_info_a_r_b}{G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+RB} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{glxproto_8h_af560d8902307c6bb79aea4900c8393fc}\label{glxproto_8h_af560d8902307c6bb79aea4900c8393fc}} 
\index{glxproto.\+h@{glxproto.\+h}!x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+R\+B\+Req@{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+R\+B\+Req}}
\index{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+R\+B\+Req@{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+R\+B\+Req}!glxproto.\+h@{glxproto.\+h}}
\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+R\+B\+Req}{xGLXSetClientInfoARBReq}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily typedef struct \hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_set_client_info_a_r_b}{G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+RB}  \hyperlink{glxproto_8h_af560d8902307c6bb79aea4900c8393fc}{x\+G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+R\+B\+Req}}

Protocol header for gl\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info\+A\+RB

This structure is follwed by {\ttfamily num\+Versions} $\ast$ 2 {\ttfamily C\+A\+R\+D32} values listing the Open\+GL versions supported by the client. The pairs of values are an Open\+GL major version followed by a minor version. For example, \begin{DoxyVerb} CARD32 versions[4] = { 2, 1, 3, 0 };
\end{DoxyVerb}


says that the client supports Open\+GL 2.\+1 and Open\+GL 3.\+0.

These are followed by {\ttfamily num\+G\+L\+Extension\+Bytes} bytes of {\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G8} containing the Open\+GL extension string supported by the client and up to 3 bytes of padding.

The list of Open\+GL extensions is followed by {\ttfamily num\+G\+L\+X\+Extension\+Bytes} bytes of {\ttfamily S\+T\+R\+I\+N\+G8} containing the G\+LX extension string supported by the client and up to 3 bytes of padding.

This protocol replaces {\ttfamily \hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_client_info}{G\+L\+X\+Client\+Info}}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_client_info}{G\+L\+X\+Client\+Info}, \hyperlink{struct_g_l_x_set_client_info2_a_r_b}{G\+L\+X\+Set\+Client\+Info2\+A\+RB} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
